class=\"owl-dot\"><span></span></div></div></div></div>\n\n\t</div>\n</div>\n\n\n<div class=\"blocked-hover pb3 pt3\" link=\"http://www.lronhubbard.org/\">\n\t<h2 class=\"mt0 pt0\">\n\t\t<a href=\"http://www.lronhubbard.org/\">\n\t\t\tL. RON HUBBARD<br>\n\t\t\t<span class=\"not-bold\">Founder of Dianetics &amp; Scientology</span>\n\t\t</a>\n\t</h2>\n\t<p>There are only two tests of a life well lived, L. Ron Hubbard once remarked: Did one do as one intended? And were people glad one lived? In testament to the first stands the full body of his life’s work, including the more than 12,000 writings and 3,000 tape-recorded lectures of Dianetics and Scientology.\n</p>\n\t<a class=\"learn-more pull-right flip\" href=\"http://www.lronhubbard.org/\" target=\"_blank\">learn more, visit:&nbsp;www.lronhubbard.org\n </a>\n</div>\n\n<div class=\"blocked-hover pb3 pt2\" link=\"/what-is-scientology.html\">\n\t<h2 class=\"mt0 pt0\">\n\t\t<a href=\"/what-is-scientology.html\">\n\t\t\tWHAT IS SCIENTOLOGY?\n<br>\n\t\t</a>\n\t</h2>\n\t<p>Scientology is a religion in its highest meaning, as it helps bring Man to total freedom and truth. The essential tenets of Scientology are these:\n </p><div class=\"pl2\"><p>You are an immortal spiritual being.</p>\n<p>Your experience extends well beyond a single lifetime. And your capabilities are unlimited, even if not presently realized.</p>\n<p>Furthermore, Man is basically good. He is seeking to survive. And his survival depends upon himself and his fellows and his attainment of brotherhood with the universe.</p>\n</div> <a class=\"learn-more pull-right flip\" href=\"/what-is-scientology.html\" target=\"_self\">learn more </a><p></p>\n</div>\n\n<div class=\"pb3 blocked-hover\" link=\"/david-miscavige/\">\n\t<h2 class=\"mt0 pt0\">\n\t\t<a href=\"/david-miscavige/\">\n\t\t\tDAVID MISCAVIGE:<br>\n\t\t\t<span class=\"not-bold\">At the Helm of Scientology’s Explosive Growth\n</span>\n\t\t</a>\n\t</h2>\n\t<p><a href=\"/david-miscavige.html?link=bodytext\">David Miscavige</a> is the ecclesiastical leader of the Scientology religion. From his position as Chairman of the Board Religious Technology Center (RTC), Mr. Miscavige bears the ultimate responsibility for ensuring the standard and pure application of L.&nbsp;Ron Hubbard’s technologies and Keeping Scientology Working.\n</p>\n\t<a class=\"learn-more pull-right flip\" href=\"/david-miscavige/\" target=\"_self\">learn more </a>\n</div>\n\n\n\n\n\n<div
